üö© 8 AM ‚ûú üèÅ 11:30 AM ‚õÖÔ∏è 47f ‚ûú üå§Ô∏è 58f üö¥üèª 39.59 mi üöµüèª 448 ft üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òï Portfolio Fit 4101 E Olympic Plaza, Long Beach, CA 90803 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Group road Ride - IBM from Santa Teresa Park Side

Please note this is the SUNDAY ride, starting from Mike's Bikes in Los Gatos. Wheels roll at 8:30. Route will head out Shannon and follow Coleman till we pass Almaden Lake Park and turn right into the neighborhoods. At mile 13 we visit Bernal-Gulnac-Joice Ranch with water/bathroom. At mile 16 we summit the north side of IBM, stopping for a quick regroup before descending the south side and heading back to Mike's Bikes. Route is 30 miles with 1,800 feet of climbing.

Group road Ride - IBM from Santa Teresa Park Side

ÂèëËµ∑‰∫∫: Mark Thompson

Âë®‰∏Ä
LGBRC MLK Day Bonus Monday Road Ride

Hi team, I am planning to lead a bonus ride for this Monday, January 20th. The ride will head up Hicks Rd from the north before stopping for a regroup (bathroom and water rest) at the Almaden Quicksilver parking lot. From there, we will paceline from McKean Rd along Uvas before turning left on Willow Springs and heading back to Los Gatos via Santa Teresa and IBM. The route is 54.5 miles with 3700 ft of elevation gain. Wheels roll at 8:35 am sharp. This is a no drop ride. I hope to see you there!

üö© 8 AM ‚ûú üèÅ 11:30 AM üå• 55f ‚ûú ‚òÄ 68f üö¥üèª 37.56 mi üöµüèª 1,832 ft üÖøÔ∏è Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 ‚òïÔ∏è Brown Sugar 26851 Aliso Creek Rd, Aliso Viejo, CA 92656 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

üö© 8 AM ‚ûú üèÅ 11:30 AM üå• 55f ‚ûú ‚òÄ 68f üö¥üèª 37.85 mi üöµüèª 490 ft üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òï Daydream 864 W 16th St, Newport Beach, CA 92663 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Road Ride OLH via Arastradero/Alpine

Hi team, This Saturday, I will lead the group to Old La Honda road in Woodside. We will meet at Mike‚Äôs Bikes in Los Gatos at 8:30 AM, wheels will roll at 8:35 AM. We will head to Old La Honda road in a counter-clockwise direction, beginning by taking Hwy9 to Pierce, followed by climbing Mt. Eden and descending down to Steven‚Äôs Canyon. We will try to keep the group together by paceline on Foothill, before turning on Arastradero Rd. We will stop for water/bathroom on Arastradero Rd before heading a bit further west into Portola Valley. We will regroup at the top of OLH before beginning our ride back to Los Gatos via Skyline and Hwy9. I will strongly advocate for keeping the group together as much as possible on Skyline Blvd. If needed, we can also stop for bathroom/water at the Skyline and Page Mill intersection. The ride is 54 miles with just over 5000ft of elevation gain. Please bring plenty of nutrition and water and remember to refuel and rehydrate throughout the ride.

Group Road Ride - Counter-clockwise IBM

Please note, this is the SUNDAY ride starting from Mike‚Äôs Bikes in Los Gatos. Wheels roll at 8:30. Non-members please fill out the waiver from the LGBRC website or fill one out electronically when you arrive at the start. Route will head out over Shannon, Hicks to Camden and into the neighborhoods at Leyland Park Dr. We will stop at the bathrooms/water on Mockingbird Hill Ln (12 miles into the ride). Then summit IBM hill before returning to Mikes Bikes. Route is roughly 30 miles, 2,200 ft of climbing.

SF3UN8 Roll out: 8 AM Coffee break: 30-40 minutes ETA back: 11:30AM ‚òÄ 49f ‚ûú ‚òÄ 64f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Pico Rivera Golf Club 3260 Fairway Dr, Pico Rivera, CA 90660 ‚òïÔ∏è Delight Pastry (16.84M) 39 N Raymond Ave, Pasadena, CA 91103 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

9Q6WS4 Roll out: 8 AM Coffee break: 30-40 minutes ETA back: 11:20AM üå• 51f ‚ûú üå§ 62f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ‚òï The Vintage 1979 9252 Garden Grove Blvd Unit 28 and 27, Garden Grove, CA 92844 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Saturday Road Ride on December 28th

Dear fellow teammates, Forecast looks promising for this Saturday and perfect for a nice endurance adventure. The plan is to climb Mt Tam and ride along the coast for some scenic views. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descents. If you are planning on joining I would ask if you could please RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride. Please notice that the route may be subject to changes as we are still refining it üòä

[LGBRC Rides] Sunday Gravel Ride on December 22nd

Dear fellow teammates, Notice that this is a parallel ride to the regular Sunday road ride offered by the club. Plan is to do a long gravel ride along two iconic parks: Calero and QuickSilver. The ride will be a bit demanding, so please do not forget to bring lots of food and water. Also notice that this ride may be cancelled in case of rain or wet terrain. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descent. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Sunday Road Ride - Calero Park

We do some nice warmup climbs and wind through the Leyland Park maze before embarking on the feature, the classic McKean Rd TT out to Calero Park, where there are restrooms and water. McKean can be a hammer fest when certain instigators (such as me) show up, but the focus this week is on collaboration and teamwork. I promise!

Roll out: 8 AM Coffee break: 30-40 minutes ETA back: 11:20AM ‚òÅ 53f ‚ûú ‚òÅ 60f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òï 1 Oz Coffee & Food (19.37M) 155 5th St Suite 121, Huntington Beach, CA 92648 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Saturday Road Ride - Ca√±ada, West OLH, Skyline Loop

We made it to the end of the year. I‚Äôm looking forward to some mellow team riding after a few months of sprinty cyclocross. Lots of paceline on the way out along Foothill and through Portola valley. First rest stop is at town hall on Portola Rd. Then onto Ca√±ada and up 92 to Skyline. A bunch of climbing, then a right turn to partially descend La Honda. Be vigilant here, as we‚Äôll be making a tricky left turn onto West Old La Honda to get back up to Skyline. Then we stay the course until Page Mill where we can take a rest room stop, then a quick water refill if needed at the fire station and finally down 9 and back to home base.

Endurance Training Ride

The proposed route is Mt Hamilton all the way out to Patterson and back. Depending on how the group feels and the weather we can assess fatigue at the top of Hamilton, and at The Junction before heading all the way into Patterson. The target pace is to finish in 8-10hrs. This is a strict no-drop ride as the route is very remote and the riders should stick together to support one another in the event of a crash or severe mechanical. With that said, if you struggle to get up Hamilton in 2.5hrs I may ask you to turn back as it will be hard to finish the ride in the time window. Be self-sufficient with navigation, basic repair supplies, food, and water. There‚Äôs water at the top of Hamilton and at The Junction. The ride will definitely finish after dark so have lights to descend Hamilton. Feel free to DM me on strava or the club WhatsApp for further details. Wheels roll at 8am

We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Eden before heading up Mt. Eden and regrouping again at the top of Pierce. Then, we'll climb Hwy 9 to the intersection of Redwood Gulch before heading back down Hwy 9 and back to the shop. Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hello team, There is a good probability that we will have rain this Sunday. If the forecast shows rain for Sunday morning, this ride will be canceled. In the event that we have dry or dry-ish conditions this Sunday, we will meet at MBLG to head south to climb and descend IBM from the same direction. Before climbing IBM, we will stop for bathroom and water at the top of Mockingbird. Wheels roll at 8:35am sharp.

PP96KV 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÅ 55f ‚ûú üå• 62f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ‚òïÔ∏è Phin Smith (18.24M) 12921 Main St, Garden Grove, CA 92840 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Sunday Ride

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes üå• 52f ‚ûú üå§ 76f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 ‚òïÔ∏è Oslo Coffee Co (21.23M) 25642 Crown Valley Pkwy Suite E1, Ladera Ranch, CA 92694 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Saturday Road Ride - On Orbit & Soda Springs

Let‚Äôs grind up some steep gradients this Saturday. We last sweated this route out in May, which necessitated an extra bottle in our jersey pockets. Conditions should be much more favorable this time, but you‚Äôll want a layer for the summits. We roll over to Saratoga, climb Bohlman the fun way (left on Norton, left on On Orbit, left on Bohlman), descend Montevina, wind around the reservoir to Soda Springs, chug up that to the gate. Then we take a little detour left on Weaver because it‚Äôs so scenic (just make sure to stop at the bottom before the driveway or you‚Äôll make friends with some dogs). Then we head back on the creek trail. Short & steep.

7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes üå• 57f ‚ûú üå§ 68f Flat Pace: 17-19mph Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òï Rye Goods (17.9M) 15771 Red Hill Ave Suite 110, Tustin, CA 92780 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Recruitment Ride (B Route)

This Saturday is our annual recruitment ride. Come ride some of our favorite haunts, then join us for gelato on the club at Dolce Spazio. We head out over Shannon to McKean, with a rest stop at Calero park. We then take Bailey up and around to IBM hill (The A group will stay on Bailey to Metcalf). After that, we wind our way to Kennedy and head back to the shop.

LGBRC Recruitment Ride (A Route)

This Saturday is our annual recruitment ride. Come ride some of our favorite haunts, then join us for gelato on the club at Dolce Spazio. We head out over Shannon to McKean, with a rest stop at Calero park. We then take Bailey up to the feature climb, Metcalf. After regrouping at the top, we‚Äôll descend the backside and loop back around to IBM hill. After that, we wind our way to Kennedy and head back to the shop. There is also alternate route for those would like to skip the Metcalf loop and go directly to IBM hill.

Group Road Ride - Up 9, down Redwood Gulch

This route is the clockwise version of the regular Redwood Gulch route (2nd Sunday of the month as of this posting). This gives us an opportunity to climb highway 9. One notable change is the out/back after the decent of Redwood Gulch on Stevens Canyon Rd, this adds an additional 4 miles to the total. Before the intersection with Mt. Eden we will stop at Cooley Picnic Area on the left for bathrooms and water. After a quick stop we continue around the reservoir and then follow neighborhood roads back to Mike‚Äôs Bikes.

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÅ 58f ‚ûú üå§ 75f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Columbus Tustin Park 14652 Prospect Ave, Tustin, CA 92780 ‚òïÔ∏è Mameya Coffee Roasters (18.95M) 27931 La Paz Rd E, Laguna Niguel, CA 92677 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

AV-C Ride Oct 26th, 2024 - Crestview via Palomar and Woodridge Climb

Meet: 9:00 AM, Leave: 9:15 AM We will be going north Saturday, and the weather forecast looks favorable. We will get up to Crestview via Palomar. There are many turns up Palomar, so just follow the signs to keep on Palomar. We have a very short regroup at the gate and a longer regroup at Crestview Park. We will follow Crestview and then Ralston to Crystal Springs with a connection to Woodridge. We will then go up Woodridge climb and connect with Black Mountain Rd. We will then head back on Skyline-Canada and the last main regroup will be at the Water Temple. Planned Regroups: Mountain Home and 84 (Woodside) Crestview Park Skyline and Golf Course Dr. Water Temple Backyard Brew Non-Members: Alto Velo welcomes non-members to join us on our rides. However, non-members must have a Waiver on file with the club. Filling out the waiver is only required one time per year. Ride Etiquette https://www.altovelo.org/ride-rules

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 26th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, Let's be back on the road and let's enjoy HW9 that has been recently reopened! The plan for this weekend is to do a classic loop: up HW9, down bear creek and up Big Basin way. As always, we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Weather forecast looks great and while temperatures will be likely on the high 70s we will probably enjoy lower temperatures while climbing: however, please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops), and do not forget to eat constantly. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

WC2PB9 6:15 AM Roll out ‚òÄÔ∏è 54f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 80f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Covina Station 600 N Citrus Ave, Covina, CA 91723 Coffee break for 20 minutes ‚òïÔ∏è Lou, The French On The Block (32.07M) 4007 W Riverside Dr, Burbank, CA 91505 Lunch break for 40 minutes üçΩ The Back Door Bakery & Cafe (69M) 8349 Foothill Blvd, Sunland, CA 91040 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Gravel Ride on October 19th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to do something different and go for a nice gravel ride: climb El Sereno, and JNT before looping around and come back to LG through the LG Creek trail. As always, we will be stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Please be gentle with me as I am still new on the dirt :-) Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Êó∂Èó¥: 8:30 AM, Saturday, OCT 19, 2024

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hi team, This Sunday's ride will approach Hicks Rd. from the South. Wheels will roll at 8:35 and take Shannon to Hicks before heading over Camden and taking the maze to New Almaden. We will stop for water and the bathroom at the New Almaden parking lot before climbing Hicks. We will regroup at the top of Hicks where there is also a bathroom at the Hicks and Umunhum intersection. We'll descend Hicks and head back to MBLG via Shannon and Kennedy.

R72UT9 7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÄÔ∏è 57f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 72f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òïÔ∏è Eller Bakery (15.30M) 1651 Placentia Ave, Costa Mesa, CA 92627 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 12th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to have a long endurance ride and after climbing Hicks, we will head to Uvas before climbing MetCalf. The plan is to keep the peloton together throughout the all ride, but as always we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Notice that the route is designed for "escapes" in case anyone may like to leave early. Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.
